height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="relative"><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼd ͼr"><div class="cm-scroller"><pre class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly m-0"><code><span># 8-Bit ALU using Verilog HDL</span><br><br><span>## Overview</span><br><span>This project implements an 8-Bit Arithmetic Logic Unit (ALU) using Verilog HDL.  </span><br><span>The ALU performs multiple arithmetic, logical, and shift operations based on the select input. The design was developed and simulated using :contentReference[oaicite:0]{index=0}.</span><br><br><span>---</span><br><br><span># Features</span><br><span>The ALU supports the following operations:</span><br><br><span>| Select Input | Operation |</span><br><span>|---|---|</span><br><span>| 0000 | Addition |</span><br><span>| 0001 | Subtraction |</span><br><span>| 0010 | AND |</span><br><span>| 0011 | OR |</span><br><span>| 0100 | XOR |</span><br><span>| 0101 | NAND |</span><br><span>| 0110 | NOR |</span><br><span>| 0111 | XNOR |</span><br><span>| 1000 | Shift Left |</span><br><span>| 1001 | Shift Right |</span><br><span>| 1010 | Increment |</span><br><span>| 1011 | Decrement |</span><br><br><span>---</span><br><br><span># ALU Architecture</span><br><br><span>## Inputs</span><br><span>- `A [7:0]` : 8-bit input A</span><br><span>- `B [7:0]` : 8-bit input B</span><br><span>- `S [3:0]` : Select line for operation selection</span><br><br><span>## Outputs</span><br><span>- `Result [7:0]` : ALU output</span><br><span>- `Carry_Borrow` : Carry/Borrow flag</span><br><span>- `Zero` : Zero flag</span><br><span>- `Overflow` : Overflow flag</span><br><br><span>---</span><br><br><span># Status Flags</span><br><br><span>## Carry/Borrow Flag</span><br><span>Indicates carry generation during addition or borrow during subtraction.</span><br><br><span>## Zero Flag</span><br><span>Becomes HIGH when the ALU result equals zero.</span><br><br><span>## Overflow Flag</span><br><span>Indicates signed arithmetic overflow.</span><br><br><span>---</span><br><br><span># Project Structure</span><br><br><span>```text</span><br><span>8bit-ALU-Verilog/</span><br><span>│</span><br><span>├── src/</span><br><span>│   └── ALU_8bit.v</span><br><span>│</span><br><span>├── tb/</span><br><span>│   └── ALU_8bit_tb.v</span><br><span>│</span><br><span>├── sim/</span><br><span>│   └── waveform.png</span><br><span>│</span><br><span>├── docs/</span><br><span>│   ├── RTL_schematic.png</span><br><span>│   └── Block_Diagram.png</span><br><span>│</span><br><span>├── README.md</span><br><span>└── LICENSE</span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<h1 data-section-id="1thb7jp" data-start="1462" data-end="1474">Simulation</h1>
<p data-start="1475" data-end="1601">Behavioral simulation was performed using Vivado Simulator.<br data-start="1534" data-end="1537">
Waveforms were verified for all ALU operations and status flags.</p>

<h1 data-section-id="tkk17o" data-start="1608" data-end="1620">How to Run</h1>

<p data-start="1632" data-end="1673">Open Vivado and create a new RTL project.</p>

<p data-start="1685" data-end="1709">Add the following files:</p>

</li>
<li data-section-id="1mx2ri1" data-start="1725" data-end="1742">
<p data-start="1727" data-end="1742"><code data-start="1727" data-end="1742">ALU_8bit_tb.v</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-section-id="18m0qh0" data-start="1744" data-end="1753">Step 3</h2>
<p data-start="1754" data-end="1758">Run:</p>

</li>

</li>

</li>
</ul>

<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1849" data-end="1886"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button type="button" class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-2cb00440.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="relative"><div class="pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼd ͼr"><div class="cm-scroller"><pre class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly m-0"><code><span>A = 15</span><br><span>B = 10</span><br><span>Result = 25</span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

data-custom-highlighting-behavior="boundary" class="A_HxFq_root" data-testid="collapsible-user-message-root" data-can-expand="" data-expanded=""><div id="_r_md_" data-testid="collapsible-user-message-content" class="A_HxFq_content"><div class="max-w-full min-w-0 [overflow-wrap:anywhere] whitespace-pre-wrap"># 8-Bit ALU using Verilog HDL

An 8-Bit Arithmetic Logic Unit (ALU) designed using Verilog HDL and simulated in Vivado.  
This ALU performs arithmetic, logical, and shift operations based on the select input signals.

---

# Project Overview

The ALU is one of the core components of a processor responsible for performing arithmetic and logical operations.  
This project demonstrates the implementation of an 8-bit ALU using combinational logic in Verilog HDL.

The design supports multiple operations such as:
- Addition
- Subtraction
- Logical Operations
- Shift Operations
- Increment/Decrement

The project was simulated and verified using Xilinx Vivado.

---

# Features

## Arithmetic Operations
- Addition
- Subtraction
- Increment
- Decrement

## Logical Operations
- AND
- OR
- XOR
- NAND
- NOR
- XNOR

## Shift Operations
- Left Shift
- Right Shift

## Status Flags
- Carry/Borrow Flag
- Zero Flag
- Overflow Flag

---

# ALU Operations Table

| Select Input (S) | Operation |
|------------------|-----------|
| 0000 | Addition |
| 0001 | Subtraction |
| 0010 | AND |
| 0011 | OR |
| 0100 | XOR |
| 0101 | NAND |
| 0110 | NOR |
| 0111 | XNOR |
| 1000 | Shift Left |
| 1001 | Shift Right |
| 1010 | Increment |
| 1011 | Decrement |

---

# Block Diagram

&lt;img width="100%" alt="8bit ALU Block Diagram" src="docs/Block_Diagram.png"&gt;

---

# Project Structure

<pre class="max-w-full min-w-0 overflow-x-auto [overflow-wrap:anywhere] whitespace-pre-wrap"><code>text
8bit-ALU-Verilog/
│
├── src/
│   └── ALU_8bit.v
│
├── tb/
│   └── ALU_8bit_tb.v
│
├── sim/
│   ├── waveform.png
│   └── simulation_output.png
│
├── docs/
│   ├── Block_Diagram.png
│   ├── RTL_Schematic.png
│   └── Project_Report.pdf
│
├── README.md
├── LICENSE
└── .gitignore</code></pre>

---

# Inputs and Outputs

## Inputs

| Signal | Size | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| A | 8-bit | First input operand |
| B | 8-bit | Second input operand |
| S | 4-bit | Operation select input |

---

## Outputs

| Signal | Size | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| Result | 8-bit | ALU operation result |
| Carry_Borrow | 1-bit | Carry/Borrow flag |
| Zero | 1-bit | Zero flag |
| Overflow | 1-bit | Overflow flag |

---

# Tools Used

- Verilog HDL
- Xilinx Vivado

---

# Simulation and Verification

The ALU functionality was verified using a Verilog testbench in Vivado Simulator.

The following were verified:
- Arithmetic operations
- Logical operations
- Shift operations
- Carry generation
- Overflow detection
- Zero flag functionality

---

# Sample Results

## Addition

<pre class="max-w-full min-w-0 overflow-x-auto [overflow-wrap:anywhere] whitespace-pre-wrap"><code>text
A = 15
B = 10
Result = 25</code></pre>

## Subtraction

<pre class="max-w-full min-w-0 overflow-x-auto [overflow-wrap:anywhere] whitespace-pre-wrap"><code>text
A = 20
B = 20
Result = 0
Zero Flag = 1</code></pre>

## Shift Left

<pre class="max-w-full min-w-0 overflow-x-auto [overflow-wrap:anywhere] whitespace-pre-wrap"><code>text
A = 00001111
Result = 00011110</code></pre>

---

# How to Run the Project

## Step 1
Open Vivado and create a new RTL project.

## Step 2
Add the following files:
- <code class="user-message-inline-code">ALU_8bit.v</code>
- <code class="user-message-inline-code">ALU_8bit_tb.v</code>

## Step 3
Run:
- Behavioral Simulation
- Synthesis
- RTL Analysis

## Step 4
Verify waveforms and RTL schematic.

---

# RTL Design Concepts Used

- Combinational Logic Design
- Case Statements
- Bitwise Operations
- Shift Operations
- Flag Generation Logic
- RTL Simulation
- Hardware Verification
 --- 

# Future Enhancements

- 16-bit ALU
- Pipelined ALU
- Multiplier and Divider Unit
- Signed Arithmetic Support
- FPGA Board Implementation

---

# Learning Outcomes

Through this project, the following skills were developed:

- Verilog HDL Coding
- RTL Design
- FPGA Design Flow
- Testbench Development
- Waveform Analysis
- Vivado Simulation and Synthesis
